************************
************************
UHLL Test Message Report
************************
************************

This report provides a full set of both outbound and inbound UHLL messages on a version by version basis.
The sections are sorted by UHLL specification version, with each section providing a full set of UHLL
messages for that version.

The messages have been formatted in such a way as to allow you to copy and paste the message(s) required for
testing, and then easily change header and DFID content to meet your needs. It is recommended that you use a
feature rich text editor (e.g. Notepad++) that supports global value changing. All messages that specifically need
to be tested may be copied and pasted to a clean text file. Content may then be globally changed to meet
the specific UHLL header DFID data needs of the test.

Here are some tips for taking advantage of the message format in this report:

o All test messages are designed to be used with the HPD Common Scripting Interface (CSI) tool. While
  CSI is recommended, you are not required to use it. You may remove the CSI directives by doing the following:

	o Change "<<" to "" to remove the CSI data flow directive.
	o Change <STX>, <ETX> and <LRC> to whatever you use for start of text, end of text and checksum, if any.

o Outbound messages (i.e. messages FROM the PMS) contain "@@@" in the UHLL message header. This is a place
  holder for the DMM of the PMS. You will need to change this to the DMM of the PMS you are testing. For example,
  change all occurrences of "@@@" to "445".

o Inbound messages (i.e. messages TO the PMS) contain "###" in the UHLL message header. This is a place
  holder for the DMM of the GSS device. You will need to change this to the DMM of the GSS you are testing.
  For example, change all occurrences of "###" to "114".

o All DFIDs contain a value that represents the name associated with the DFID number (e.g. 106014Account Number,
  175011Room Number, etc.). This has been done to:

	o Prevent the need to have to constantly refer to the UHLL specification to determine the meaning of a DFID number.
	o Allow a DFID value to be globally changed for any given test. For example, change all occurrences of
	  "175011Room Number" to "17500310A" so that all messages in your test are for room 10A.

o Please refer to the Message Definition Table below for a summary of message names and their associated numbers.

	o Not all messages are available in all versions of UHLL.
	o Message definitions may vary by UHLL version.
	o Please refer to the online UHLL specification for the version(s) required for more information.

A new version of this report will be published, in tandem, with all future revisions of UHLL. Please remember
to visit the HPD website (https://my.comtrol.com) to download the latest version of this report.
